  353 alex_action_5 = plain          TReserved
  354 alex_action_6 = plain          TPunct
  355 alex_action_7 = plain          TOp
  356 alex_action_8 = plain          TVar
  357 alex_action_9 = xform read'    TLit
  358 alex_action_10 = xform readCode TCode
  359 alex_action_11 = xform readCode TCType
  360 alex_action_12 = addon read'    TNum
  361 alex_action_13 = addon readBin  TNum
  362 alex_action_14 = addon read'    TNum
  363 alex_action_15 = addon read'    TNum
  364 alex_action_16 = plain          TUnknown
  365 
  366 #define ALEX_GHC 1
  367 #define ALEX_NOPRED 1
  368 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  369 -- ALEX TEMPLATE
  370 --
  371 -- This code is in the PUBLIC DOMAIN; you may copy it freely and use
  372 -- it for any purpose whatsoever.

  374 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  375 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  376 
  377 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  378 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  379 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  380 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  381 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  382 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  383 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  384 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  385 #  else
  386 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  387 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  388 #  endif
  389 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  390 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  391 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  392 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  393 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  394 #else
  395 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  396 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  397 #  define FAST_INT Int
  398 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  399 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  400 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  401 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  402 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  403 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  404 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  405 #endif
  406 
  407 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  408 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  409 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  410 
  411 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
  412 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  413 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  414 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  415   narrow16Int# i
  416   where
  417         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
  418         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  419         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  420         off' = off *# 2#
  421 #else
  422 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  423   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
  424 #endif
  425     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
  426 #endif
  427 #else
  428 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  429 #endif
  430 
  431 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  432 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
  433 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  434 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  435 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  436   narrow32Int# i
  437   where
  438    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
  439                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
  440                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
  441    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
  442    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
  443    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  444    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  445    off' = off *# 4#
  446 #else
  447 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  448   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
  449 #endif
  450     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
  451 #endif
  452 #else
  453 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  454 #endif
  455 
  456 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  457 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
  458 quickIndex = unsafeAt
  459 #else
  460 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
  461 #endif
  462 
  463 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  464 -- Main lexing routines
  465 
  466 data AlexReturn a
  467   = AlexEOF
  468   | AlexError  !AlexInput
  469   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
  470   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
  471 
  472 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
  473 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
  474   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
  475 
  476 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
  477   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  478   (AlexNone, input__') ->
  479     case alexGetByte input__ of
  480       Nothing ->
  481 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  482                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
  483 #endif
  484                                    AlexEOF
  485       Just _ ->
  486 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  487                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
  488 #endif
  489                                    AlexError input__'
  490 
  491   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
  492 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  493     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
  494 #endif
  495     AlexSkip input__'' len
  496 
  497   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
  498 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  499     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
  500 #endif
  501     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
  502 
  503 
  504 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
  505 -- state it encountered.
  506 
  507 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
  508   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
  509   let
  510   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
  511   in
  512   new_acc `seq`
  513   case alexGetByte input__ of
  514      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
  515      Just (c, new_input) ->
  516 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  517       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
  518 #endif
  519       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
  520         let
  521                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
  522                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
  523 
  524                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
  525                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
  526                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
  527                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
  528                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
  529         in
  530         case new_s of
  531             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
  532                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
  533                 -- character that failed, not after.
  534             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
  535 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
  536                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
  537                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
  538 #else
  539                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
  540                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
  541 #endif
  542                    new_input new_s new_acc
  543       }
  544   where
  545         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
  546         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  547         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
  548 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  549         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
  550            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  551            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  552            | otherwise
  553            = check_accs rest
  554         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
  555            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  556            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
  557            | otherwise
  558            = check_accs rest
  559 #endif
  560 
  561 data AlexLastAcc
  562   = AlexNone
  563   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
  564   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
  565 
  566 data AlexAcc user
  567   = AlexAccNone
  568   | AlexAcc Int
  569   | AlexAccSkip
  570 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  571   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  572   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  573 
  574 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
  575 
  576 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  577 -- Predicates on a rule
  578 
  579 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
  580   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
  581 
  582 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
  583 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
  584 
  585 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
  586 
  587 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
  588 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
  589 
  590 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
  591 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
  592      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  593           (AlexNone, _) -> False
  594           _ -> True
  595         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
  596         -- match when checking the right context, just
  597         -- the first match will do.
  598 #endif
  599 {-# LINE 107 "src/SAWScript/Lexer.x" #-}
  600 -- token helpers
  601 
  602 plain ::                   (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  603 xform :: (Text -> Text) -> (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  604 addon :: (Text -> a) -> (Pos -> Text -> a -> Token Pos) -> Pos -> Text -> Token Pos
  605 
  606 plain   tok pos txt = tok pos txt         -- ^ just the contents
  607 xform f tok pos txt = tok pos (f txt)     -- ^ transform contents
  608 addon f tok pos txt = tok pos txt (f txt) -- ^ also variant contents
  609 
  610 -- fetch a value via Read
  611 --
  612 -- XXX: we should not use this for string literals, because as much as
  613 -- it's convenient to have the stdlib decode escape sequences for us,
  614 -- the escape sequences available in SAWScript strings should properly
  615 -- be defined by SAWScript (that is, explicitly here) and not by
  616 -- what's in GHC's standard library.
  617 --
  618 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to get the source position into the panic
  619 -- message in case it ever actually happens, but that seems difficult
  620 -- to arrange.
  621 read' :: Read a => Text -> a
  622 read' txt = case readMaybe txt' of
  623     Just x -> x
  624     Nothing -> panic "Lexer" ["Failed to decode string or number literal", txt']
  625   where txt' = Text.unpack txt
  626 
  627 -- drop the {{ }} or {| |} from Cryptol blocks
  628 readCode :: Text -> Text
  629 readCode txt = Text.drop 2 $ Text.dropEnd 2 txt
  630 
  631 -- read a binary integer
  632 readBin :: Text -> Integer
  633 readBin s = case readInt 2 isDigit cvt (Text.unpack s') of
  634               [(a, "")] -> a
  635               _         -> error $ "Cannot read a binary number from: " ++ show s
  636   where cvt c = ord c - ord '0'
  637         isDigit c = c == '0' || c == '1'
  638         s' | "0b" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  639            | "0B" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  640            | True                     = s
  641 
  642 
  643 -- alex support and lexer mechanism
  644 
  645 -- current position
  646 data AlexPos = AlexPos {
  647     apLine :: !Int,
  648     apCol :: !Int
  649   }
  650 
  651 -- input state
  652 type AlexInput = (
  653     AlexPos,    -- ^ Current position
  654     Text        -- ^ Remaining input
  655   )
  656 
  657 -- initial position
  658 startPos :: AlexPos
  659 startPos = AlexPos { apLine = 1, apCol = 1 }
  660 
  661 -- feed alex a byte describing the current char
  662 -- this came from Cryptol's lexer, which came from LexerUtils, which
  663 -- adapted the technique used in GHC's lexer.
  664 byteForChar :: Char -> Word8
  665 byteForChar c
  666   | c <= '\7' = non_graphic
  667   | Char.isAscii c = fromIntegral (ord c)
  668   | otherwise = case Char.generalCategory c of
  669       Char.LowercaseLetter       -> lower
  670       Char.OtherLetter           -> lower
  671       Char.UppercaseLetter       -> upper
  672       Char.TitlecaseLetter       -> upper
  673       Char.DecimalNumber         -> digit
  674       Char.OtherNumber           -> digit
  675       Char.ConnectorPunctuation  -> symbol
  676       Char.DashPunctuation       -> symbol
  677       Char.OtherPunctuation      -> symbol
  678       Char.MathSymbol            -> symbol
  679       Char.CurrencySymbol        -> symbol
  680       Char.ModifierSymbol        -> symbol
  681       Char.OtherSymbol           -> symbol
  682       Char.Space                 -> sp
  683       Char.ModifierLetter        -> other
  684       Char.NonSpacingMark        -> other
  685       Char.SpacingCombiningMark  -> other
  686       Char.EnclosingMark         -> other
  687       Char.LetterNumber          -> other
  688       Char.OpenPunctuation       -> other
  689       Char.ClosePunctuation      -> other
  690       Char.InitialQuote          -> other
  691       Char.FinalQuote            -> tick
  692       _                          -> non_graphic
  693   where
  694   -- CAUTION: these must match the $uni* values at the top of the file
  695   non_graphic     = 0
  696   upper           = 1
  697   lower           = 2
  698   digit           = 3
  699   symbol          = 4
  700   sp              = 5
  701   other           = 6
  702   tick            = 7
  703 
  704 -- input handler for alex
  705 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Word8, AlexInput)
  706 alexGetByte (pos, text) = fmap doGet $ Text.uncons text
  707     where
  708       doGet (c, text') = (byteForChar c, (move pos c, text'))
  709       move pos c = case c of
  710           '\n' -> AlexPos { apLine = apLine pos + 1, apCol = 1 }
  711           _ -> pos { apCol = apCol pos + 1 }
  712 
  713 -- the lexer we're generating doesn't use this hook
  714 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  715 alexInputPrevChar _ = panic "Lexer" ["alexInputPrevChar"]
  716 
  717 -- read the text of a file, passing in the filename for use in positions
  718 scanTokens :: FilePath -> Text -> [Token Pos]
  719 scanTokens filename str = go (startPos, str)
  720   where
  721     fillPos pos height width =
  722         let startLine = apLine pos
  723             startCol = apCol pos
  724             endLine = startLine + height
  725             endCol = startCol + width
  726         in
  727         Range filename startLine startCol endLine endCol
  728 
  729     go inp@(pos, str) = case alexScan inp 0 of
  730         AlexEOF ->
  731             let pos' = fillPos pos 0 0 in
  732             [TEOF pos' "EOF"]
  733         AlexError (pos, _) ->
  734             let line' = show $ apLine pos
  735                 col' = show $ apCol pos
  736             in
  737             error $ line' ++ ":" ++ col' ++ ": unspecified lexical error"
  738         AlexSkip inp' len ->
  739             go inp'
  740         AlexToken inp' len act ->
  741             let text = Text.take len str
  742                 (height, width) = case reverse $ Text.lines text of
  743                     [] -> (0, 0)
  744                     [line] -> (0, Text.length line)
  745                     last : lines -> (length lines, Text.length last)
  746                 pos' = fillPos pos height width
  747             in
  748             act pos' text : go inp'
  749 
  750 -- | State for processing comments.
  751 --
  752 -- CNone is the ground state (not in a comment)
  753 --
  754 -- CBlock startpos n is when we're within a block comment starting at
  755 -- startpos, and n is the number of additional nested block comments
  756 -- that have been opened.
  757 --
  758 -- CLine is when we're in a line (//-type) comment.
  759 data CommentState = CNone | CBlock Pos !Int | CLine
  760 
  761 -- | Type to hold a diagnostic message (error or warning).
  762 --
  763 -- This should cease to be needed once we clean out the message
  764 -- printing infrastructure. It's here only to shorten the type
  765 -- signatures below, and represents the possibility of having
  766 -- generated a message.
  767 type OptMsg = Maybe (Verbosity, Pos, Text)
  768 
  769 -- | Postprocess to drop comments; this allows block comments to nest.
  770 --
  771 -- Also returns a message (error or warning) along with the updated
  772 -- token list if there's an unclosed comment when we reach EOF. Since
  773 -- we aren't in a monad here and can't print, dispatching the message
  774 -- is the caller's responsibility.
  775 dropComments :: [Token Pos] -> ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  776 dropComments = go CNone
  777   where go :: CommentState -> [Token Pos] -> ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  778         go state ts = case ts of
  779           [] ->
  780             -- should always see TEOF before we hit the end
  781             panic "Lexer" ["dropComments: tokens ran out"]
  782           TEOF _ _ : _ : _ ->
  783             -- should only see TEOF at the end of the list
  784             panic "Lexer" ["dropComments: misplaced EOF in tokens"]
  785 
  786           t : ts' ->
  787             let take state' =
  788                     let (results, optmsg) = go state' ts' in
  789                     (t : results, optmsg)
  790                 drop state' = go state' ts'
  791                 finish = ([t], Nothing)
  792                 finishWith msg = ([t], Just msg)
  793             in
  794             case state of
  795               CNone -> case t of
  796                 TEOF _ _ ->
  797                     -- plain EOF
  798                     finish
  799                 TCommentS pos _ ->
  800                     -- open block-comment
  801                     drop (CBlock pos 0)
  802                 TCommentL _ _  ->
  803                     -- begin line-comment
  804                     drop CLine
  805                 TEOL _ _ ->
  806                     -- ordinary EOL, doesn't need to be seen downstream; drop it
  807                     drop CNone
  808                 _ ->
  809                     -- uncommented token, keep it
  810                     take CNone
  811 
  812               CBlock startpos depth -> case t of
  813                 TEOF pos _ ->
  814                     -- EOF in /**/-comment; unclosed, which is an error
  815                     finishWith (Error, startpos, "Unclosed block comment")
  816                 TCommentS _ _ ->
  817                     -- open nested comment, keep original start position
  818                     drop (CBlock startpos (depth + 1))
  819                 TCommentE _ _
  820                  | depth == 0 ->
  821                      -- end outer block comment
  822                      drop CNone
  823                  | otherwise ->
  824                      -- end nested block comment
  825                      drop (CBlock startpos (depth - 1))
  826                 _ ->
  827                      -- anything else in a block comment, drop it
  828                      -- (this includes any TCommentLs that come through)
  829                      drop state
  830 
  831               CLine -> case t of
  832                 TEOF pos _ ->
  833                     -- EOF in //-comment; missing a newline
  834                     finishWith (Warn, pos, "Missing newline at end of file")
  835                 TEOL _ _ ->
  836                     -- EOL ending a line comment, drop it
  837                     -- (EOLs aren't sent downstream)
  838                     drop CNone
  839                 _ ->
  840                     -- anything else in a line comment, drop it
  841                     -- (this includes any TCommentS/TCommentE that appear)
  842                     drop CLine
  843 
  844 -- entry point
  845 lexSAW :: FilePath -> Text -> ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  846 lexSAW f text = dropComments $ scanTokens f text
  847 
  848 -- alternate monadic entry point (XXX: does this have any value?)
  849 scan :: Monad m => FilePath -> Text -> m ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  850 scan f = return . lexSAW f
